HE THOUGHT TOO THAT ALTHOUGH HE SHOULD SPEND THREE OR EVEN FOUR YEARS IN THAT OCCUPATION YET THESE ADDED TO THE FEW HE THEN COUNTED WOULD NOT MAKE HIM SO OLD BUT THAT HE MIGHT AFTERWARDS RETURN TO HIS STUDIES
THUS I AM NOT A POET BUT ONLY A LOVER OF POETRY
I SAY IT IS NEITHER SEEMLY NOR PROPER THAT THIS DAMSEL SHOULD LIVE IN AN INN
FOUR DAYS AFTERWARDS RICHARD SET OUT ON HIS EXILE AND THE MONEY HAD BEEN ALREADY PAID
THE DAY AFTER THE ARRIVAL OF THE PILGRIMS MARCO ANTONIO'S FATHER CELEBRATED THE MARRIAGES OF HIS SON AND TEODOSIA DON RAFAEL AND LEOCADIA WITH EXTRAORDINARY MAGNIFICENCE
BUT THIS SENOR MUST FIRST OF ALL SWEAR THAT WHEN HE IS INSIDE HERE HE WILL NOT ATTEMPT TO DO ANYTHING BUT SING AND PLAY WHEN HE IS ASKED AND THAT HE WILL KEEP CLOSE AND QUIET WHEREVER WE MAY PUT HIM I SWEAR TO THIS SAID LOAYSA
GIVE THYSELF UP WHOLLY TO THE CAPRICIOUS BOY ON WHOM THY GAZE IS FIXED SO THAT LOSING ALL HOPE OF WINNING THEE I MAY LOSE TOO THE LIFE I ABHOR
AND FINDING THEMSELVES OPPOSITE EACH OTHER HE WHO APPEARED TO BE THE ELDER SAID TO THE YOUNGER OF WHAT COUNTRY IS YOUR WORSHIP NOBLE SIR AND BY WHAT ROAD DO YOU PROPOSE TO TRAVEL WHAT IS MY COUNTRY SENOR CAVALIER RETURNED THE OTHER I KNOW NOT
HOW SUCH A PERFECT CHRYSOLITE COULD HUMBLE MANZANARES YIELD
WELL I KNOW WITHOUT MY HELP YOU CAN NOT SECURE ME
MY MISTRESS SAYS SHE WEARS HAIR-CLOTH NEXT HER SKIN HIGHLY DELIGHTED WITH WHAT HE HAD HEARD FROM THE GALLEGAN THE GENTLEMAN DID NOT WAIT TILL THEY HAD TAKEN OFF HIS SPURS BUT CALLED FOR THE LANDLORD AND WITHDREW WITH HIM INTO A PRIVATE ROOM
THE LANDLORD IMMEDIATELY LOOKED ABOUT FOR HIS ASS AND SAW IT IN THE HANDS OF ANOTHER CATCHPOLL WHO HAD JOINED THE ALGUAZIL'S PARTY
LOPE THEN RELATED HOW THE BOYS ANNOYED HIM CALLING AFTER HIM FOR THE TAIL AND TOMAS ADVISED HIM NOT TO GO ABROAD AT LEAST WITH HIS ASS OR IF HE DID THAT HE SHOULD CHOOSE ONLY THE LEAST FREQUENTED STREETS
BY THIS YOU MAY JUDGE SIGNORA THROUGH WHAT TROUBLES I HAVE HAD TO PASS SINCE BEING WHAT I AM I HAVE BEEN BROUGHT TO SERVE AS THE HOUSEKEEPER OF SPANIARDS OR AS WHAT THEY CALL THEIR GOUVERNANTE
FOR I WAS AS MODEST AND AS VIRTUOUS AS ANY MAIDEN IN THE WORLD AND YET I HAVE DONE WHAT I HAVE TOLD YOU
AND AS THERE WAS NO NEED TO DISCUSS THE QUESTION OF WAGES THE MORISCO SOON HAD A SERVANT AND I A MASTER
AS FOR MAKING THE SIGN OF THE CROSS WITH COPPER MONEY THAT LADIES YOU MUST KNOW LESSENS THE LUCK AT LEAST IT DOES MINE
FOR I WOULD HAVE YOU TO KNOW THAT I HAVE AN EXTRAORDINARY KNACK IN TEACHING
MOREOVER I WON'T BE PAID IN MONEY FOR THE TAIL AT SO MUCH A POUND BUT I WILL HAVE IT IN SUBSTANCE AND CUT OFF FROM THE ASS AS I HAVE SAID THE WINNER OF THE FOUR QUARTERS AND THE REST OF THE COMPANY BEGAN TO THINK THAT IT WOULD NOT BE ADVISABLE TO RESORT TO FORCE IN THIS BUSINESS FOR LOPE SEEMED TO THEM TO BE A MAN OF SUCH METTLE THAT HE WOULD NOT BE VANQUISHED WITHOUT SOME TROUBLE
BY ALL THAT YOU MOST REVERE I ENTREAT YOU TO LEAVE ME SHUT UP HERE AND LET NO ONE BEHOLD ME WHILE YOU RETURN IN ALL HASTE TO THE PLACE WHERE YOU FOUND ME AND SEE IF THERE BE ANY PERSONS FIGHTING THERE
THIS GIRL HAVING SEEN THE GIPSIES DANCE THE DEVIL POSSESSED HER TO FALL IN LOVE WITH ANDREW TO THAT DEGREE THAT SHE PROPOSED TO TELL HIM OF IT AND TAKE HIM FOR A HUSBAND IF HE WOULD HAVE HER IN SPITE OF ALL HER RELATIONS
I OUGHT NOT TO HAVE GONE FORTH UNTIL HE HAD COME TO THE DOOR
RICHARD LENT A FAVOURABLE EAR TO THIS REQUEST AND IMMEDIATELY CALLED A COUNCIL OF HIS OFFICERS TO CONSIDER WHAT MIGHT BE THE BEST MEANS OF SENDING ALL THE CHRISTIANS TO SPAIN WITHOUT INCURRING ANY RISK FROM THEM SHOULD THEIR NUMBERS ENCOURAGE THEM TO RISE AND ATTEMPT TO OVERPOWER HIS CREWS
I STROVE FOR HER LIBERATION AND VENTURED MORE FOR HER THAN FOR MY OWN LIFE
SHE IS ALMOST A CHILD TOO
AND FINALLY THE ALMOST INEVITABLE CONSEQUENCES OF ALL THIS
THEY ARE NOT WASTED BY WAR OR EXCESSIVE TOIL
NO TOM-CAT EVER PERSECUTED ITS RATS NOR WAS THE BARKING OF A DOG EVER HEARD WITHIN ITS WALLS
AFTER THEY HAD ENJOYED A SUMPTUOUS REPAST CARRIAZO RELATED TO HIS FATHER HOW FOR LOVE OF COSTANZA DON TOMAS HAD TAKEN SERVICE AS HOSTLER IN THE INN AND HOW HIS DEVOTION TO HER WAS SUCH THAT BEFORE HE KNEW HER TO BE A LADY AND THE DAUGHTER OF A MAN OF SUCH QUALITY HE WOULD GLADLY HAVE MARRIED HER EVEN AS A SCULLERY-MAID
FOR THERE IS A CURE FOR EVERY SORROW
IT WAS CARRIED INTO EFFECT AT ONCE
FOR AS HE DID NOT SIN THROUGH MALICE IT MAY BE THAT HEAVEN IN ITS GRACE WILL SEND HIM SAFETY THE CORREGIDOR WAS STILL MORE SURPRISED TO HEAR SUCH LANGUAGE FROM THE GITANILLA'S LIPS AND BUT THAT HE WOULD NOT BETRAY SIGNS OF WEAKNESS HE COULD HAVE WEPT WITH HER
BUT FANCYING THAT THEY REGARDED HIM WITH SUSPICION ESPECIALLY LORENZO HE DETERMINED TO PURSUE THE HIGHWAY AND REJOIN HIS FRIEND IN FERRARA WHERE HE WAS CERTAIN TO FIND HIM WITH BUT LITTLE DIFFICULTY
AND THAT YOU SAY IT AND THAT I HEAR IT CAUSES ME FRESH ADMIRATION AND WONDER
DEATH TILL MY MASTER ANNOYED BY MY LOUD LAMENTATIONS THREATENED ME WITH A GREAT STICK IF I DID NOT HOLD MY TONGUE
I WAS CONFOUNDED BY THIS SAD TURN OF AFFAIRS THE MANAGER WAS INCENSED THE PLAYERS VERY MERRY
SHE HAD PENDENTS IN HER EARS WHICH SEEMED TO BE PEARLS BUT WERE ONLY GLASS
HERE RODAJA BEHELD THAT VERY CHAMBER OF THE VIRGIN WHEREIN WAS DELIVERED THE MOST STUPENDOUS EMBASSY EVER HEARD OR WITNESSED BY ALL THE HEAVENS ALL THE ANGELS AND ALL THE ARCHANGELS OR OTHER INHABITANTS OF THE EVERLASTING ABODES
BUT INDEED THEY MUST BE HALF OUT IN THE RECKONING
ONE HAD A DUDGEON-DAGGER BY HIS SIDE
HE MAY DO IT FOR SAKE OF THE GRIEF BEYOND IMAGINATION WHICH THE PARENTS SUFFER FROM THE MURDER OF THEIR CHILDREN
THEY THEN ROSE BOTH OF THEM EAGER TO SEE COSTANZA BUT THE ONE ONLY FROM CURIOSITY THE OTHER FROM LOVE
THE TIME HAD NOW ARRIVED WHEN THE STUDIES OF HIS MASTERS WERE COMPLETED AND THEY RETURNED TO THEIR BIRTHPLACE WHICH WAS ONE OF THE MOST IMPORTANT CITIES OF ANDALUSIA
I TOLD MY MASTER TO TAKE MEASURES FOR POSSESSING HIMSELF OF THE MAIDEN AND THAT I WOULD GIVE HIM FOR HER RANSOM ALONE TEN THOUSAND GOLD CROWNS
JUST SO WITH THE PARCHMENT
IT WERE BETTER FOR ME TO BE PROTECTED IN HELL THAN TO REMAIN ANY LONGER WITH THAT LION AMONG SHEEP AND SHEEP AMONG MEN
AND I FOUND IN IT REMINISCENCES OF EVENTS I SHALL NEVER FORGET AS LONG AS I LIVE
I'LL TELL YOU WHAT IS TO BE DONE SAID HE
PRECIOSA REJOICED NOT A LITTLE TO SEE HER TENDER LOVER BECOME SUCH A SMART AND HANDY THIEF
BUT THE TWO FRIENDS LAYING HANDS PROMPTLY THE ONE ON HIS DUDGEON DAGGER AND THE OTHER ON HIS YELLOW HANDLED KNIFE GAVE THE MULETEER SO MUCH TO DO THAT IF HIS COMPANIONS HAD NOT HASTENED TO ASSIST HIM HE WOULD HAVE COME BADLY OUT OF THE QUARREL
NEVERTHELESS I ACCEPT IT IN ORDER TO CHASTISE YOUR INSOLENCE SO SAYING HE LEFT THE WINDOW AND CALLED FOR HIS ARMS
AND WHAT MAKES THE MIRACLE GREATER IS THAT WE NOT ONLY SPEAK BUT HOLD INTELLIGENT DISCOURSE AS THOUGH WE HAD SOULS CAPABLE OF REASON
AS ILL LUCK WOULD HAVE IT CLEMENT WAS NOT ON THE SPOT HAVING GONE FORWARD WITH SOME BAGGAGE AND ANDREW WAS SET UPON BY SO MANY THAT THEY OVERPOWERED HIM AND LOADED HIM WITH HEAVY CHAINS
BUT THAT WHEN SHE HAD ASKED IF HE WERE FABIO HE HAD ANSWERED YES AND THAT SHE HAD ENTRUSTED THE BABE TO HIS CARE IN THE FAITH OF THAT REPLY
